patterns in Envoy and Kubernetes. The implementation spans multiple layers in each project.\\n\\n## Envoy Rate Limiting Architecture\\n\\n**Local Rate Limiting** is implemented across multiple components:\\n\\n1. **HTTP Local Rate Limit Filter** (source/extensions/filters/http/local_ratelimit/): The Filter class implements Http::PassThroughFilter and intercepts requests. It uses FilterConfig to manage the rate limiter instance and calls decodeHeaders() to check if requests should be rate limited. The config holds LocalRateLimiterImpl which implements the actual token bucket logic.\\n\\n2. **Network Local Rate Limit Filter** (source/extensions/filters/network/local_ratelimit/): The Filter class implements Network::ReadFilter and enforces rate limiting at the connection level via onNewConnection(). The SharedRateLimitSingleton manages shared rate limiters across multiple configurations, using a node_hash_map to store weak pointers to LocalRateLimiterImpl instances keyed by configuration and token bucket parameters.\\n\\n3. **Common Local Rate Limit Implementation** (source/extensions/filters/common/local_ratelimit/): LocalRateLimiterImpl implements the core rate limiting logic with requestAllowed() method that consults RateLimitTokenBucket instances. It supports:\\n   - Static token buckets via default_token_bucket_\\n   - Dynamic descriptor-based buckets through DynamicDescriptorMap\\n   - Descriptor matching and LRU cache management through DynamicDescriptor\\n   - Share provider support for distributed bucket sharing across Envoy instances\\n\\n**Global Rate Limit Service Client** (source/extensions/filters/http/rate_limit_quota/): This implements a gRPC-based rate limiting quota service:\\n\\n- GlobalRateLimitClientImpl handles bidirectional streaming with the RLQS (Rate Limit Quota Service) server\\n- LocalRateLimitClientImpl provides thread-local access to global resources without locks\\n- The architecture uses thread-local storage (TLS) to safely access GlobalRateLimitClientImpl from worker threads\\n- RateLimitQuotaFilter applies the quota enforcement on HTTP requests\\n- QuotaBucketCache maintains bucket state with quota assignments and fallback behavior\\n\\nThe call chain flows: Filter::decodeHeaders() → FilterConfig::requestAllowed() → LocalRateLimiterImpl::requestAllowed() → RateLimitTokenBucket::consume()\\n\\n## Kubernetes Rate Limiting Architecture\\n\\n**Token Bucket Implementation** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/flowcontrol/throttle.go):\\n\\nKubernetes provides a token bucket rate limiter using golang.org/x/time/rate.Limiter as the underlying mechanism. NewTokenBucketRateLimiter() creates instances with configurable QPS (queries per second) and burst size. The tokenBucketRateLimiter struct wraps rate.Limiter and provides TryAccept() for non-blocking checks and Accept()/Wait() for blocking operations.\\n\\n**API Priority and Fairness (APF)** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/):\\n\\n1. **APF Filter Interface** (apf_filter.go): The Interface defines the core contract with Handle(), Run(), Install(), and tracking methods. The New() factory creates instances configured with informer factories and server concurrency limits. Handle() method orchestrates request queuing and dispatch.\\n\\n2. **APF Controller** (apf_controller.go): The configController maintains eventual consistency with PriorityLevelConfiguration and FlowSchema objects from the API. It manages priorityLevelState objects keyed by name, each containing:\\n   - Reference to the PriorityLevelConfiguration object\\n   - Per-priority-level statistics and state\\n   - Queue set management for fair queueing\\n   - Seat borrowing logic for dynamic concurrency allocation\\n\\n3. **HTTP Handler** (priority-and-fairness.go): WithPriorityAndFairness() creates an HTTP handler middleware. The priorityAndFairnessHandler implements the actual rate limiting logic:\\n   - Extracts request info and user identity\\n   - Calls noteFn callback to classify the request into a FlowSchema and PriorityLevelConfiguration\\n   - Invokes workEstimator to determine request work (seat count)\\n   - Routes to the configController's Handle() method for queueing and dispatch\\n   - Tracks execution counts for read-only vs mutating requests\\n\\n4. **Bootstrap Configuration** (default-internal.go): MandatoryPriorityLevelConfigurations and SuggestedPriorityLevelConfigurations are pre-defined bootstrap configurations. NewAPFScheme() creates a runtime.Scheme configured for flowcontrol API types.\\n\\n5. **Data Types** (staging/src/k8s.io/api/flowcontrol/v1/types.go): PriorityLevelConfiguration represents the API object with:\\n   - Type field (Exempt or Limited)\\n   - Limited configuration specifying nominalConcurrencyShares and queueing behavior\\n   - LimitedPriorityLevelConfiguration specifies how to handle queuing and request fairness\\n\\nThe call chain flows: priorityAndFairnessHandler::Handle() → configController::Handle() → queueing and seat allocation logic\\n\\nBoth implementations share the common pattern of using token buckets for rate limiting, but Kubernetes APF adds sophisticated priority-based queue management and fair queueing to provide adaptive concurrency control at the API server level.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3427,"cache_read_input_tokens":93619,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3427},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"28227a3a-1f52-4e8f-9f5d-b74b29451db8","uuid":"7011f571-9400-4351-972d-9446e53dda0e"}

patterns in Envoy and Kubernetes. The implementation spans multiple layers in each project.\\n\\n## Envoy Rate Limiting Architecture\\n\\n**Local Rate Limiting** is implemented across multiple components:\\n\\n1. **HTTP Local Rate Limit Filter** (source/extensions/filters/http/local_ratelimit/): The Filter class implements Http::PassThroughFilter and intercepts requests. It uses FilterConfig to manage the rate limiter instance and calls decodeHeaders() to check if requests should be rate limited. The config holds LocalRateLimiterImpl which implements the actual token bucket logic.\\n\\n2. **Network Local Rate Limit Filter** (source/extensions/filters/network/local_ratelimit/): The Filter class implements Network::ReadFilter and enforces rate limiting at the connection level via onNewConnection(). The SharedRateLimitSingleton manages shared rate limiters across multiple configurations, using a node_hash_map to store weak pointers to LocalRateLimiterImpl instances keyed by configuration and token bucket parameters.\\n\\n3. **Common Local Rate Limit Implementation** (source/extensions/filters/common/local_ratelimit/): LocalRateLimiterImpl implements the core rate limiting logic with requestAllowed() method that consults RateLimitTokenBucket instances. It supports:\\n   - Static token buckets via default_token_bucket_\\n   - Dynamic descriptor-based buckets through DynamicDescriptorMap\\n   - Descriptor matching and LRU cache management through DynamicDescriptor\\n   - Share provider support for distributed bucket sharing across Envoy instances\\n\\n**Global Rate Limit Service Client** (source/extensions/filters/http/rate_limit_quota/): This implements a gRPC-based rate limiting quota service:\\n\\n- GlobalRateLimitClientImpl handles bidirectional streaming with the RLQS (Rate Limit Quota Service) server\\n- LocalRateLimitClientImpl provides thread-local access to global resources without locks\\n- The architecture uses thread-local storage (TLS) to safely access GlobalRateLimitClientImpl from worker threads\\n- RateLimitQuotaFilter applies the quota enforcement on HTTP requests\\n- QuotaBucketCache maintains bucket state with quota assignments and fallback behavior\\n\\nThe call chain flows: Filter::decodeHeaders() → FilterConfig::requestAllowed() → LocalRateLimiterImpl::requestAllowed() → RateLimitTokenBucket::consume()\\n\\n## Kubernetes Rate Limiting Architecture\\n\\n**Token Bucket Implementation** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/flowcontrol/throttle.go):\\n\\nKubernetes provides a token bucket rate limiter using golang.org/x/time/rate.Limiter as the underlying mechanism. NewTokenBucketRateLimiter() creates instances with configurable QPS (queries per second) and burst size. The tokenBucketRateLimiter struct wraps rate.Limiter and provides TryAccept() for non-blocking checks and Accept()/Wait() for blocking operations.\\n\\n**API Priority and Fairness (APF)** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/flowcontrol/):\\n\\n1. **APF Filter Interface** (apf_filter.go): The Interface defines the core contract with Handle(), Run(), Install(), and tracking methods. The New() factory creates instances configured with informer factories and server concurrency limits. Handle() method orchestrates request queuing and dispatch.\\n\\n2. **APF Controller** (apf_controller.go): The configController maintains eventual consistency with PriorityLevelConfiguration and FlowSchema objects from the API. It manages priorityLevelState objects keyed by name, each containing:\\n   - Reference to the PriorityLevelConfiguration object\\n   - Per-priority-level statistics and state\\n   - Queue set management for fair queueing\\n   - Seat borrowing logic for dynamic concurrency allocation\\n\\n3. **HTTP Handler** (priority-and-fairness.go): WithPriorityAndFairness() creates an HTTP handler middleware. The priorityAndFairnessHandler implements the actual rate limiting logic:\\n   - Extracts request info and user identity\\n   - Calls noteFn callback to classify the request into a FlowSchema and PriorityLevelConfiguration\\n   - Invokes workEstimator to determine request work (seat count)\\n   - Routes to the configController's Handle() method for queueing and dispatch\\n   - Tracks execution counts for read-only vs mutating requests\\n\\n4. **Bootstrap Configuration** (default-internal.go): MandatoryPriorityLevelConfigurations and SuggestedPriorityLevelConfigurations are pre-defined bootstrap configurations. NewAPFScheme() creates a runtime.Scheme configured for flowcontrol API types.\\n\\n5. **Data Types** (staging/src/k8s.io/api/flowcontrol/v1/types.go): PriorityLevelConfiguration represents the API object with:\\n   - Type field (Exempt or Limited)\\n   - Limited configuration specifying nominalConcurrencyShares and queueing behavior\\n   - LimitedPriorityLevelConfiguration specifies how to handle queuing and request fairness\\n\\nThe call chain flows: priorityAndFairnessHandler::Handle() → configController::Handle() → queueing and seat allocation logic\\n\\nBoth implementations share the common pattern of using token buckets for rate limiting, but Kubernetes APF adds sophisticated priority-based queue management and fair queueing to provide adaptive concurrency control at the API server level.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
